   <value name="body"><![CDATA[This class, Mod Loader, is the first one into the game
and handels everything in the first scene where the
player is on the aircraft carrier.

Before this plan this was split into 3 different classes, 
but became a pain when managing so they are now 
all in one class.

This class can be split into 3 sections.
Singleplayer Mod Loading/Downloading and dealing
with the buttons on that page.
Multiplayer picking pilot and vehicle, joining the server,
displaying the lobby information or displaying a ban and
then taking you to the next scene.
Lastly Setup, which creates the asset bundle which as the 
items we need to create our mod UI, moves the old ui and
sets up all the buttons for the vr controller to use.
]]></value>

   <value name="body"><![CDATA[This gets placed on all the networked players vehicle, and listens 
for the tag which gets sent from the server then moves their ai
depending on what information got sent.

The NetworkingManager class just sets client, worldCenter, player 
and id then calls SetReceiver and leaves this class to do what it 
needs to do.

This class finds the needed scripts to apply the information sent
from the server in the Start method. When the message is 
received and the ID matches, it first stores all the information 
sent into the players class, then calls UpdateAI which fetches it 
from that player class to update this AI.]]></value>
